# awesome-machine-learning-startups
List of 2632 startups doing AI &amp; ML across 42 cities. Built automatically, hence unreliable. Not vibe-coded. Inspired by [this](https://github.com/jrieke/awesome-machine-learning-startups-berlin). 

Fields: üëÅ Computer Vision, üìö Natural Language Processing, ü§ñ Robotics, üíâ Medicine, üöó Self-Driving Cars, üó£ Voice & Sound, ü§ñ Chatbots & Customer Service, üßæ Document Processing, üîé Search & Recommendation, üî¨ Science & Engineering, üí∞ Business, üëî Consulting, üöÄ Other 

Jump to: [Amsterdam](#amsterdam), [Austin](#austin), [Bangalore](#bangalore), [Barcelona](#barcelona), [Beijing](#beijing), [Berlin](#berlin), [Boston](#boston), [Chicago](#chicago), [Copenhagen](#copenhagen), [Dublin](#dublin), [Eindhoven](#eindhoven), [Gurgaon](#gurgaon), [Helsinki](#helsinki), [Hyderabad](#hyderabad), [Lausanne](#lausanne), [London](#london), [Los-angeles](#los-angeles), [Madrid](#madrid), [Milan](#milan), [Mumbai](#mumbai), [Munich](#munich), [New-york](#new-york), [Palo-alto](#palo-alto), [Paris](#paris), [Pune](#pune), [Rotterdam](#rotterdam), [San-francisco](#san-francisco), [Seattle](#seattle), [Seoul](#seoul), [Shanghai](#shanghai), [Shenzhen](#shenzhen), [Singapore](#singapore), [Stockholm](#stockholm), [Sydney](#sydney), [Taichung](#taichung), [Taipei](#taipei), [Tel-aviv](#tel-aviv), [Tokyo](#tokyo), [Toronto](#toronto), [Turin](#turin), [Vienna](#vienna), [Zurich](#zurich)
